Tully_1 = {
	name = Hoster # Canon
	dynasty = dynn_Tully

	dna = Tully_1

	martial = 4
	diplomacy = 4
	intrigue = 4
	stewardship = 4
	learning = 4
	prowess = 7

	religion = the_seven_main
	culture = riverlander
	sexuality = heterosexual

	father = Tully_67
	mother = Tully_rs_7

	trait = education_diplomacy_4
	trait = patient
	trait = gregarious
	trait = diligent
	trait = authoritative
	trait = bossy

	disallow_random_traits = yes

	8239.1.1 = { 
		birth = yes 
		add_character_flag = canon_status_canon
	}
	8255.1.1 = {
		trait = knight
		trait = strong
	}
	8260.1.1 = {
		effect = {
			if = { 
				limit = { character:Baelish_1 = { is_alive = yes } }
				set_relation_friend = {
					target = character:Baelish_1 # Corwyn Baelish
					reason = friend_saved_life # War of the Ninepenny Kings
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8263.1.1 = {
		add_spouse = Whent_6 # Minisa Whent
		effect = {
			if = { 
				limit = { character:Whent_6 = { is_alive = yes } }
				set_relation_lover = {
					target = character:Whent_6 # Minisa Whent
					reason = lover_spouse
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8280.1.2 = {
		trait = widowed
		create_character_memory = {
			type = lover_died
			participants = {
				dead_relation = character:Whent_6 # Minisa Whent
			}
		}
	}
	8282.9.15 = { # Robert's Rebellion
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { game_start_date = 8282.9.15 }
				add_character_flag = bookmark_independent
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { character:Frey_1 = { is_alive = yes } }
				add_opinion = {
					modifier = hate_opinion
					target = character:Frey_1 # Walder Frey
					opinion = -40
				}
				reverse_add_opinion = {
					modifier = hate_opinion
					target = character:Frey_1 # Walder Frey
					opinion = -40
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				0 = {
					modifier = {
						add = agot_historic_event_chance
					}
				}
				0 = {
					modifier = {
						add = agot_nonhistoric_event_chance
					}
					create_story = story_agot_widowed
						random_owned_story = {
						limit = {
							story_type = story_agot_widowed
						}
						set_variable = {
							name = dead_lover
							value = character:Whent_6
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8284.1.1 = { # Crowned Stag
		effect = {
			remove_variable = pre_war_liege
		}
	}
	8296.1.1 = { trait = ill }
	8299.1.1 = { 
		effect = { add_trait = infirm } # Becomes bedridden, but still lucid
	}
	8299.5.1 = { 
		effect = { 
			remove_trait = infirm 
			add_trait = incapable # Mind continues to slip more and more
		}
	}
	8299.10.1 = { 
		trait = incapable
		death = yes 
	}
}

				every_dynasty_member = {

						target = ROOT

					}

						target = ROOT

					}

						target = ROOT
